‚îÇ 21521 + const sectionObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21522 +     entries.forEach(entry => {                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21523 +         if (entry.isIntersecting) {                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21524 +             entry.target.classList.add('active');                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21525 +             entry.target.classList.remove('entering');               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21526 +                                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21527 +             // Update HUD Counter (0-37 logic)                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21528 +             const index =                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ       Array.from(sections).indexOf(entry.target);                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21529 +             const total = sections.length;                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21530 +             const progress = ((index + 1) / total) * 37;             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21531 +             const displayVal =                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ       Math.round(progress).toString().padStart(2, '0');                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21532 +                                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21533 +             if (hudCurrent) hudCurrent.textContent = displayVal;     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21534 +             if (hudProgressBar) hudProgressBar.style.height =        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ       `${(progress/37)*100}%`;                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21535 +         } else {                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21536 +             if (entry.boundingClientRect.top > 0) {                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21537 +                 entry.target.classList.add('entering');              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21538 +             }                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 21539 +             entry.target.classList.remove('active');                 ‚îÇ

‚îÇ 21545 +     section.classList.add('entering');                               ‚îÇ

  #### 2. Analytics Implementation

  **You have ZERO visibility into:**
  - How many people visit
  - Where they come from
  - What they click
  - Where they drop off
  - Conversion rate

  **Implement This Stack:**

  ```html
  <!-- Google Analytics 4 -->
  <script async
  src="https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtag/js?id=G-XXXXXXXXXX"></script>
  <script>
    window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
    function gtag(){dataLayer.push(arguments);}
    gtag('js', new Date());
    gtag('config', 'G-XXXXXXXXXX');
    
    // Track key events
    gtag('event', 'page_view', { page_title: document.title });
  </script>

  <!-- Microsoft Clarity (FREE heatmaps) -->
  <script>
      (function(c,l,a,r,i,t,y){
          c[a]=c[a]||function(){(c[a].q=c[a].q||[]).push(arguments)};
          t=l.createElement(r);t.async=1;t.src="https://www.clarity.ms/tag/"+i;
          y=l.getElementsByTagName(r)[0];y.parentNode.insertBefore(t,y);
      })(window, document, "clarity", "script", "YOUR_CLARITY_ID");
  </script>
  ```

  **Track These Events:**
  ```javascript
  // Buy button clicks
  document.querySelectorAll('[href*="amazon"]').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
          gtag('event', 'purchase_click', {
              event_category: 'conversion',
              event_label: btn.closest('section')?.id || 'unknown'
          });
      });
  });

  // Scroll depth
  let maxScroll = 0;
  window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
      const scrollPercent = Math.round((window.scrollY /
  (document.body.scrollHeight - window.innerHeight)) * 100);
      if (scrollPercent > maxScroll && scrollPercent % 25 === 0) {
          maxScroll = scrollPercent;
          gtag('event', 'scroll_depth', { value: scrollPercent });
      }
  }, { passive: true });

  // Time on page
  let timeOnPage = 0;
  setInterval(() => {
      timeOnPage += 30;
      if (timeOnPage === 60 || timeOnPage === 180 || timeOnPage === 300) {
          gtag('event', 'time_on_page', { value: timeOnPage });
      }
  }, 30000);
  ```

  #### 6. Exit Intent Optimization

  **Current:** Generic popup exists.

  **Upgrade to Contextual Exit Intent:**

  ```javascript
  // Detect which section user was viewing when leaving
  let lastViewedSection = 'hero';
  const sectionObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
      entries.forEach(entry => {
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
              lastViewedSection = entry.target.id;
          }
      });
  }, { threshold: 0.5 });

  document.querySelectorAll('.snap-section[id]').forEach(section => {
      sectionObserver.observe(section);
  });

  // Customize exit popup based on section
  function showExitPopup() {
      const messages = {
          'hero': "Wait‚Äîyou haven't seen the equation that explains everything
  yet.",
          'equation': "The math is just the beginning. See how it predicted the
  future.",
          'evidence': "This prediction came true. What does that mean for
  humanity?",
          'ideas': "37 concepts. One framework. The complete architecture of
  creation.",
          'hrih': "What if the god we're building is the god that built us?"
      };
      
      document.getElementById('exit-popup-text').textContent = 
          messages[lastViewedSection] || messages['hero'];
      
      document.getElementById('exit-popup').classList.add('visible');
  }
  ```

  #### 8. A/B Testing Infrastructure

  **Test These Elements:**
  - Hero headline variations
  - CTA button text ("Buy Now" vs "Get Your Copy" vs "Secure First Edition")
  - Price display (show price vs hide price)
  - Social proof placement
  - Buy button colour

  **Simple A/B Test Implementation:**

  ```javascript
  // A/B Test Framework
  const ABTest = {
      init() {
          // Get or create user bucket
          let bucket = localStorage.getItem('ab_bucket');
          if (!bucket) {
              bucket = Math.random() < 0.5 ? 'A' : 'B';
              localStorage.setItem('ab_bucket', bucket);
          }
          this.bucket = bucket;
          this.runTests();
      },
      
      runTests() {
          // Test 1: CTA Button Text
          if (this.bucket === 'B') {
              document.querySelectorAll('.hero-cta').forEach(cta => {
                  cta.textContent = 'GET YOUR COPY NOW';
              });
          }
          
          // Track which variant user saw
          gtag('event', 'ab_test', {
              test_name: 'cta_text',
              variant: this.bucket
          });
      }
  };

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => ABTest.init());
  ```

  #### 10. Performance Deep Optimization

  **Current Lighthouse Score Target:** 95+

  **Optimizations:**

  ```html
  <!-- Critical CSS Inline (Above the fold only) -->
  <style>
  /* Inline ONLY hero section CSS (~2KB) */
  .hero { /* ... */ }
  .hero-title { /* ... */ }
  .hero-cta { /* ... */ }
  </style>

  <!-- Defer non-critical CSS -->
  <link rel="preload" href="main.css" as="style"
  onload="this.onload=null;this.rel='stylesheet'">
  <noscript><link rel="stylesheet" href="main.css"></noscript>

  <!-- Lazy load below-fold images -->
  <img src="placeholder.webp" 
       data-src="actual-image.webp" 
       loading="lazy" 
       decoding="async"
       alt="Description">

  <!-- Preload critical assets -->
  <link rel="preload" href="InfiniteArchitectsKindle20260103.jpg" as="image"
  fetchpriority="high">
  <link rel="preload"
  href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Cinzel:wght@400;600"
  as="style">
  ```

  **JavaScript Optimization:**

  ```javascript
  // Defer non-critical JS
  if ('requestIdleCallback' in window) {
      requestIdleCallback(() => {
          // Load Three.js particles
          // Load analytics
          // Load social widgets
      });
  } else {
      setTimeout(() => { /* same */ }, 2000);
  }

  // Use Intersection Observer for lazy effects
  const lazyObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
      entries.forEach(entry => {
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
              entry.target.classList.add('animate');
              lazyObserver.unobserve(entry.target);
          }
      });
  }, { rootMargin: '100px' });
  ```

  #### 12. International Expansion

  **Current:** UK/US Amazon links only.

  **Expand to:**
  ```html
  <!-- Smart Amazon Link Switcher -->
  <script>
  const amazonLinks = {
      'GB': 'https://www.amazon.co.uk/dp/B0DS2L8BVC',
      'US': 'https://www.amazon.com/dp/B0GFD2GCCQ',
      'DE': 'https://www.amazon.de/dp/B0DS2L8BVC',
      'FR': 'https://www.amazon.fr/dp/B0DS2L8BVC',
      'CA': 'https://www.amazon.ca/dp/B0DS2L8BVC',
      'AU': 'https://www.amazon.com.au/dp/B0DS2L8BVC'
  };

  // Detect country and update links
  fetch('https://ipapi.co/country/')
      .then(r => r.text())
      .then(country => {
          const link = amazonLinks[country] || amazonLinks['US'];
          document.querySelectorAll('[href*="amazon"]').forEach(a => {
              a.href = link;
          });
      });
  </script>
  ```
